[TYPE] "Default"
  RequiresPreciseTargeting No       // Means can be used without the precise location info
  CanBeUsedAgainst Ground // can attack this unit type
  CanBeUsedAgainst Naval
  CanBeUsedAgainst City
  CanBeUsedAgainst AbstractPosition

[TYPE] "SemiGuided" ///Like Default but can't be used against abstract position. i.e. units only
  RequiresPreciseTargeting No
  CanBeUsedAgainst Ground
  CanBeUsedAgainst Naval 
  Affects City

[TYPE] "No Attack"
  RequiresPreciseTargeting Yes
  
[TYPE] "LandAttack"
  RequiresPreciseTargeting No
  CanBeUsedAgainst Ground
  Affects City

[TYPE] "Nuke"
  RequiresPreciseTargeting No
  CanBeUsedAgainst Ground
  CanBeUsedAgainst Naval
  CanBeUsedAgainst City
  CanBeUsedAgainst AbstractPosition
  Affects Airborne // CanBeUsedAgainst automatically triggers Affects
  Affects Subwater
  DrawNuke
//  Affects Missile

[TYPE] "Torpedo"
  RequiresPreciseTargeting No
  Subwater Yes
  CanBeUsedAgainst Naval
  CanBeUsedAgainst Subwater
  
[TYPE] "TorpedoNuke"
  RequiresPreciseTargeting No
  Subwater Yes
  CanBeUsedAgainst Naval
  CanBeUsedAgainst AbstractPosition

  Affects Ground

[MISSILE] "Free fall bomb"
  Tech "M_Free_fall_bomb"
  Type "Default"
  Icon "Units/Images/Missiles/bomb.png"
  Movie "Units/Images/Projectiles/Bomb_Conventional.midx"
  Model "Units/Images/Projectiles/Model/Bomb_Conventional.MIDX"
  DrawSize 3
  DrawBomb
  Explosion "std_bomb"
  Range 50 // Bomb Range
  Ballistic
  FreeFalling
  Precision 1.75 // this is the potential deviation from the target
  CanBeLimited false
    ///Causes collateral damage
  AffectedBy Unit "Collateral_Damage_Modifier" Damage 1500000 ///Small Munition Damage

  AIHint CounterValue 0 //Default Conventional
  AIHint CounterForce 1 //Default Conventional
